local function v68() -- name: updUI
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_62, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_63
	local v64 = script.Parent.Upgrade
	local v65 = v_u_62.Value
	local v66 = v65 + 100
	local v67 = v_u_4.InventoryUpgradePrices[v66]
	if v67 then
		v64.Txt.Text = "<font color = \'#ffffff\'>" .. v65 .. "</font><font color = \'#cfcfcf\'> \226\134\146 </font><font color = \'#6dff5f\'>" .. v66 .. "</font> <font color = \'#ffffff\'>Slots</font>"
		v64.price.Text = v_u_34(v67) .. "\240\159\146\142"
		if v_u_63.Value < v67 then
			v64.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
		else
			v64.BackgroundTransparency = 0
		end
	else
		v64.Active = false
		v64.Txt.Text = "MAX"
		v64.price.Text = ""
		return
	end
end

	end
end

--- PlayerGui/MainGui/Pages/Rocket/MainFrame/RocketLocal/RocketModule ---
local v1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local v_u_23 = {
	["SimpleNumber"] = function(p11) -- name: SimpleNumber
		local v12 = tostring(p11)
		repeat
			local v13
			v12, v13 = string.gsub(v12, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")
		until v13 == 0
		return v12
	end,
	["InventoryFrame"] = function(p14) -- name: InventoryFrame
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_5
		if p14:GetAttribute("Delay") then
			task.wait(p14:GetAttribute("Delay"))
			if p14.Parent ~= v_u_10 then
				return
			end
		end
		if p14:GetAttribute("Unique") then
			return
		else
			local v15 = p14.Name
			if v_u_2.Gifts[v15].Price > 100 then
				if not v_u_2.Gifts[v15].Limited then
					local v_u_16 = script.InventoryFrame:Clone()
					v_u_16.LayoutOrder = v_u_2.Gifts[v15].Price
					v_u_16.Txt.Text = v15
					v_u_16.Price.Text = "\226\173\144 " .. v_u_23.SimpleNumber(v_u_2.Gifts[v15].Price)
					v_u_16.ImageLabel.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_2.Gifts[v15].Image
					v_u_16.Parent = v_u_5
					p14.Destroying:Connect(function()
						-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16
						v_u_16:Destroy()
					end)
					return v_u_16.Button
				end
			end
		end
	end,
	["Shake"] = function() -- name: Shake
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_7
		while true do
			task.wait(0.1)
			v_u_3:Create(v_u_7, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
				["Rotation"] = -2
			}):Play()
			task.wait(0.1)
			v_u_3:Create(v_u_7, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
				["Rotation"] = 2
			}):Play()
		end
	end,
	["Lines"] = function() -- name: Lines
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_3
		while true do
			task.wait(0.5)
			task.spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
				local v17 = Instance.new("Frame")
				v17.Size = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, 0, 0)
				v17.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
				local v18 = UDim2.new(math.random() + 0.6, 0, math.random() - 0.6, 0)
				v17.Position = v18
				v17.Rotation = 45
				v17.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				v17.Parent = v_u_6:WaitForChild("FakeRocket")
				local v19 = math.random(150, 190) / 350
				v_u_3:Create(v17, TweenInfo.new(1), {
					["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0
				}):Play()
				v_u_3:Create(v17, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
					["Size"] = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, v19, 0),

				}):Play()
				task.wait(0.7)
				v_u_3:Create(v17, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {
					["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1
				}):Play()
				game.Debris:AddItem(v17, 0.3)
			end)
		end
	end,
	["Mult"] = function() -- name: Mult
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
		local v20 = 100
		while true do
			task.wait(0.2)
			v20 = v20 + 4
			v_u_8.Text = "x" .. string.format("%.2f", math.ceil(v20) / 100)
		end
	end,
	["CreateSound"] = function(p21) -- name: CreateSound

			v22.Parent = v_u_9
			v22:Play()
			game.Debris:AddItem(v22, v22.TimeLength)
			return v22
		end
	end
}
return v_u_23

function TableFormat(p54, p55) -- name: TableFormat
	local v56 = {}
	for v57, v58 in ipairs(p54) do
		if v57 ~= p55 then
			table.insert(v56, v58)
		end
	end
	return v56
end

		if not v_u_63 then
			if v_u_62[v_u_64] then
				v_u_62 = TableFormat(v_u_62, v_u_64)
				v_u_27()
			end
		end
	end)
	v_u_65.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_62, (copy) v_u_64, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_65
		if v_u_62[v_u_64] then
			v_u_5:Create(v_u_65.Delete, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
				["ImageTransparency"] = 0.3
			}):Play()

		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_65
		v_u_5:Create(v_u_65.Delete, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
			["ImageTransparency"] = 1
		}):Play()
	end)
end

			if string.split(v_u_62[1].Name, " (")[1] == string.split(p66.Name, " (")[1] then
				if #v_u_62 < 5 then
					local v67 = v_u_62
					table.insert(v67, p66)
				end
			else
				v_u_62 = { p66 }
			end
		else
			v_u_62 = { p66 }
		end
		v_u_27()
	end
end
local function v72(p_u_69) -- name: ItemFrame
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_63, (copy) v_u_68
	if p_u_69:GetAttribute("Delay") then
		task.wait(p_u_69:GetAttribute("Delay"))
		if p_u_69.Parent ~= v_u_7 then
			return
		end
	end
	if p_u_69:GetAttribute("Unique") then
		return
	else
		local v70 = p_u_69.Name
		if v_u_6.Gifts[v70].Price >= 10000 then
			local v_u_71 = script.InventoryFrame:Clone()
			v_u_71.Name = p_u_69.Name
			v_u_71.Txt.Text = v70
			v_u_71.Price.Text = "\226\173\144 " .. v_u_3.SimpleNumber(v_u_6.Gifts[v70].Price)
			v_u_71.ImageLabel.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v70].Image
			v_u_71.Parent = v_u_11
			v_u_71.Limited.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[v70].Limited
			v_u_71.Winter.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_69.Name].Winter
			v_u_71.Summer.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_69.Name].Summer
			p_u_69.Destroying:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_71
				v_u_71:Destroy()

--- PlayerGui/MainGui/Pages/Tasks/MainFrame/Timer/LocalScript ---
local v1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("_DayT")
while true do
	task.wait(1)
	local v2 = v1.Value + 86400 - os.time()
	local v3 = v2 / 3600
	local v4 = math.floor(v3)
	local v5 = v2 % 3600 / 60
	local v6 = math.floor(v5)
	local v7 = v2 % 60
	if v7 < 10 then
		v7 = "0" .. v7
	end
	if v6 < 10 then
		v6 = "0" .. v6
	end
	script.Parent.Text = "Reset in: " .. v4 .. ":" .. v6 .. ":" .. v7
end

--- PlayerGui/MainGui/Pages/Tasks/MainFrame/WeeklyTimer/LocalScript ---
local v1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("_WeekT")
while true do
	task.wait(1)
	local v2 = v1.Value + 604800 - os.time()
	local v3 = v2 / 3600
	local v4 = math.floor(v3)
	local v5 = v2 % 3600 / 60
	local v6 = math.floor(v5)
	local v7 = v2 % 60
	if v7 < 10 then
		v7 = "0" .. v7
	end
	if v6 < 10 then
		v6 = "0" .. v6
	end
	script.Parent.Text = "Reset in: " .. v4 .. ":" .. v6 .. ":" .. v7
end

	if v_u_14 == "Cirque" then
		v16.LayoutOrder = -1
	end
	v16.Txt.Text = v_u_14
	for v17, v18 in v15 do
		local v19 = v16:FindFirstChild("Item" .. v17)
		v19.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_2.Gifts[v18[1]].Image
		v19.Chance.Text = v18[2] .. "%"
	end
	v16.Button.Activated:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_8
		if not v_u_11 then
			v_u_12 = v_u_14
			for _, v20 in v_u_8.Folder:GetChildren() do
				if v20:IsA("Frame") then
					v20.UIStroke.Enabled = v20.Name == v_u_12
				end
			end
		end
	end)
	v16.Parent = v_u_8.Folder
end
v_u_9.Spin.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_6
	if v_u_11 then
		return
	elseif v_u_13 then
		return
	else
		v_u_13 = true
		task.delay(0.3, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13
			v_u_13 = false
		end)
		if v_u_12 then
			local v21, v_u_22 = v_u_4.Arcade:InvokeServer(v_u_12)
			if v21 then
				v_u_11 = true
				v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_5.UI_BattleCount, v_u_7.Parent)
				local v_u_23 = {}
				for _, v24 in v_u_2.Banners[v_u_12] do
					local v25 = v24[1]
					table.insert(v_u_23, v25)
					local v26 = v24[1]
					table.insert(v_u_23, v26)
				end
				table.insert(v_u_23, "Diamond")
				table.insert(v_u_23, "Diamond")
				for v_u_27 = 1, 3 do
					task.spawn(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_27, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_23, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_7
						local v28 = v_u_9.SpinZone["Spin" .. v_u_27].RollFrame
						for _, v29 in v28:GetChildren() do
							if v29:IsA("Frame") then
								v29:Destroy()
							end
						end
						v28.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, -7 - v_u_27, 0)
						for v30 = 1, 50 do
							local v31 = v_u_3.ArcadeRandom(v_u_12) or "Diamond"
							local v32 = script.Roll:Clone()
							if v30 == 3 then
								if v_u_22 then
									v31 = v_u_22
								else
									v31 = v_u_3.ArcadeRandom(v_u_12) or "Diamond"
									while not table.find(v_u_23, v31) do
										v31 = v_u_3.ArcadeRandom(v_u_12) or "Diamond"
									end
									table.remove(v_u_23, table.find(v_u_23, v31))
								end
							end
							v32.Icon.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_2.Gifts[v31].Image
							v32.Price.Text = "\226\173\144 " .. v_u_3.SimpleNumber(v_u_2.Gifts[v31].Price)
							v32.Parent = v28
						end
						v_u_6:Create(v28, TweenInfo.new(v_u_27 / 2 + 1.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
							["Position"] = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, -0.575, 0)
						}):Play()
						task.wait(v_u_27 / 2 + 1.3)
						v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_5.UI_Tick, v_u_7.Parent)
						v_u_6:Create(v28.Parent.White, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {
							["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0.5
						}):Play()
						task.wait(0.15)
						v_u_6:Create(v28.Parent.White, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
							["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1
						}):Play()
					end)
				end
				task.wait(3.3)
				if v_u_22 then
					v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_5.UI_BattleWin, v_u_7.Parent)
				end
				v_u_11 = false
			else
				v_u_3.Notify("ERROR", v_u_22, v_u_5.UI_Error)
			end
		else
			v_u_3.Notify("ERROR", "Choose a banner", v_u_5.UI_Error)
			return
		end
	end
end)

				if v_u_18 < 10 then
					v_u_18 = v_u_18 + 1
					v_u_19.Count.Text = "x" .. v_u_18
					v_u_17.Text = "\238\128\130" .. v_u_5.SimpleNumber(v_u_10[v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case")][v_u_18])
				end
			end)
			v_u_19.Minus.Activated:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_19, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_12
				if v_u_18 > 1 then
					v_u_18 = v_u_18 - 1
					v_u_19.Count.Text = "x" .. v_u_18
					v_u_17.Text = "\238\128\130" .. v_u_5.SimpleNumber(v_u_10[v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case")][v_u_18])
				end

			local v20 = v_u_12:FindFirstChild("ID").Value

				local v21, v22 = v_u_8:InvokeServer()
				if not v21 then
					v_u_5.Notify("INFO", "You already own Premium Pass!", v_u_6.UI_Error)

					v_u_2:PromptGamePassPurchase(v_u_9, v21)
					return
				end
			else
				if v_u_12:GetAttribute("Pass") then

							if v23 then
								local v24 = game.Players:GetPlayerByUserId(v_u_9:GetAttribute("Gifting"))
								if v24 then
									v_u_11 = true
									task.delay(0.5, function()
										-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_11
										v_u_11 = false
									end)
									if v_u_7.IsPlayerOwnsGamepass:InvokeServer(v24, v20) then
										v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v23)
									else
										v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "The player already owns this gamepass", v_u_6.UI_Error)
									end
								else
									v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v23)
									return
								end
							else
								v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "This gamepass cannot be gifted", v_u_6.UI_Error)
								return
							end
						end
					else
						local v25 = v_u_9:FindFirstChild("_" .. v20)
						if v25 and v25.Value == 1 or v_u_2:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(v_u_9.UserId, v20) then
							v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "You already owns this gamepass", v_u_6.UI_Error)
						else
							v_u_2:PromptGamePassPurchase(v_u_9, v20)
						end
					end
				end
				if v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case") then
					v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v_u_4.PaidCases[v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case")][v_u_18])
					return
				end
				v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v20)
			end
		end)
	end
end

		v_u_89.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_89
			if v_u_89.Parent.Visible == true and os.time({
				["year"] = 2026,
				["month"] = 6,
				["day"] = 30,
				["hour"] = 0,
				["min"] = 0,
				["sec"] = 0
			}) - os.time() > 0 then
				game.ReplicatedStorage.Events.SkipLevel:FireServer()
			end
		end)
	end
end

				end
			end)
		end
	end
end
local function v_u_107(p101) -- name: formatReward
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8
	local v102
	if p101[1] == "snow" then
		v102 = "Snowflakes"
	elseif p101[1] == "gems" then
		v102 = "Gems"
	elseif p101[1] == "ton" then
		v102 = "TON"
	elseif p101[1] == "stars" then
		v102 = "Stars"
	elseif p101[1] == "x2" then
		v102 = "x2 Luck Potion"
	elseif p101[1] == "x4" then
		v102 = "x4 Luck Potion"
	else
		local v103 = p101[2]
		v102 = tostring(v103)
	end
	if p101[1] == "x2" or p101[1] == "x4" then
		local v104 = p101[2] or 1
		return v102 .. " (" .. tostring(v104) .. "sec)", "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
	end
	if p101[1] == "item" then
		return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[p101[2]].Image
	end
	if p101[2] then
		local v105 = v_u_8.SimpleNumber
		local v106 = p101[2]
		v102 = v102 .. " (x" .. tostring(v105(v106)) .. ")"
	end
	return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
end

local v_u_131 = os.time({
	["year"] = 2026,
	["month"] = 7,
	["day"] = 25,
	["hour"] = 0,
	["min"] = 0,
	["sec"] = 0
})
local function v_u_141() -- name: update
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_131, (copy) v_u_11
	local v132 = v_u_131 - os.time()
	if v132 <= 432000 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 48, 51)
	elseif v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
		return
	end
	local v133 = v132 / 86400
	local v134 = math.floor(v133)
	local v135 = v132 % 86400 / 3600
	local v136 = math.floor(v135)
	local v137 = v132 % 3600 / 60
	local v138 = math.floor(v137)
	local v139 = v132 % 60
	local v140 = math.floor(v139)
	v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = string.format("Ends in: %02d:%02d:%02d:%02d", v134, v136, v138, v140)
	if v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
	end
end

--- PlayerGui/MainGui/Pages/Battlepass/MainFrame/Frame/Level/Progress/Percentage/ProgressScript ---
local v_u_1 = script.Parent.Parent.Frame1
local v_u_2 = script.Parent.Parent.Frame2
function FramePosChanger(p3, p4) -- name: FramePosChanger
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_2
	if p3 == "Vertical" then
		v_u_1.Position = p4 == "Up" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(1, 0)
		v_u_2.Position = p4 == "Up" and UDim2.fromScale(1, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 0)
		v_u_1.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Up" and Vector2.new(0, 0) or Vector2.new(1, 0)
		v_u_2.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Up" and Vector2.new(1, 0) or Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_1.Size = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1)
		v_u_2.Size = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.Position = p4 == "Up" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(1, 0)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.Position = p4 == "Up" and UDim2.fromScale(1, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 0)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Up" and Vector2.new(0, 0) or Vector2.new(1, 0)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Up" and Vector2.new(1, 0) or Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.Size = UDim2.fromScale(2, 1)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.Size = UDim2.fromScale(2, 1)
	elseif p3 == "Horizontal" then
		v_u_1.Position = p4 == "Right" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 1)
		v_u_2.Position = p4 == "Right" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 1) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 0)
		v_u_1.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Right" and Vector2.new(0, 0) or Vector2.new(0, 1)
		v_u_2.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Right" and Vector2.new(0, 1) or Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_1.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 0.5)
		v_u_2.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 0.5)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.Position = p4 == "Right" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 0) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 1)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.Position = p4 == "Right" and UDim2.fromScale(0, 1) or UDim2.fromScale(0, 0)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Right" and Vector2.new(0, 0) or Vector2.new(0, 1)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.AnchorPoint = p4 == "Right" and Vector2.new(0, 1) or Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_1.ImageLabel.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 2)
		v_u_2.ImageLabel.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 2)
	end
end
function Progress(p5) -- name: Progress
	if p5 == 0 then
		script.Parent.Parent.Frame1.ImageLabel.Visible = false
		script.Parent.Parent.Frame2.ImageLabel.Visible = false
	else
		script.Parent.Parent.Frame1.ImageLabel.Visible = true
		script.Parent.Parent.Frame2.ImageLabel.Visible = true
	end
	local v6 = script.Parent.Parent.AbsoluteSize.X + 0.5
	local _ = math.floor(v6) % 2
	local v7 = script.Parent.Parent.AbsoluteSize.Y + 0.5
	local _ = math.floor(v7) % 2
	local v8 = p5 * 3.6
	local v9 = math.clamp(v8, 0, 360)
	local v10 = script.Parent.Parent.Frame1.ImageLabel
	local v11 = script.Parent.Parent.Frame2.ImageLabel
	local v12 = v10.UIGradient
	local v13 = v11.UIGradient
	v10.ImageColor3 = script.ImageColor.Value
	v11.ImageColor3 = script.ImageColor.Value
	v10.ImageTransparency = script.ImageTrans.Value
	v11.ImageTransparency = script.ImageTrans.Value
	v10.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. script.ImageId.Value
	v11.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. script.ImageId.Value
	if script.StarterPoint.Value == "Up" or script.StarterPoint.Value == "Down" then
		FramePosChanger("Vertical", script.StarterPoint.Value)
		if script.StarterPoint.Value == "Up" then
			if script.Direction.Value == "Left" then
				local v14 = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v13, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = math.clamp(v9, 0, 180)
				})
				v14:Play()
				v14.Completed:Wait()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v12, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = math.clamp(v9, 180, 360)
				}):Play()
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Right" then
				local v15 = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v12, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = 180 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 180)
				})
				v15:Play()
				v15.Completed:Wait()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v13, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = -math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) + 180
				}):Play()
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Middle" then
				local v16 = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v12, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = 180 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2
				})
				v16:Play()
				v16.Completed:Wait()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v13, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
					["Rotation"] = math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2
				}):Play()
			end
		elseif script.StarterPoint.Value == "Down" then
			if script.Direction.Value == "Left" then
				v12.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) + 180
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 180) + 180
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Right" then
				v12.Rotation = -math.clamp(v9, 0, 180)
				v13.Rotation = -math.clamp(v9, 180, 360)
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Middle" then
				v12.Rotation = -math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2 + 180
			end
		end
	elseif script.StarterPoint.Value == "Left" or script.StarterPoint.Value == "Right" then
		FramePosChanger("Horizontal", script.StarterPoint.Value)
		if script.StarterPoint.Value == "Left" then
			if script.Direction.Value == "Left" then
				v12.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) - 90
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 180) - 90
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Right" then
				v12.Rotation = 90 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 180)
				v13.Rotation = -math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) + 90
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Middle" then
				v12.Rotation = 90 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2 - 90
			end
		elseif script.StarterPoint.Value == "Right" then
			if script.Direction.Value == "Left" then
				v12.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) + 90
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 180) + 90
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Right" then
				v12.Rotation = 270 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 180)
				v13.Rotation = -math.clamp(v9, 180, 360) + 270
			elseif script.Direction.Value == "Middle" then
				v12.Rotation = 270 - math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2
				v13.Rotation = math.clamp(v9, 0, 360) / 2 + 90
			end
		end
	else
		script.StarterPoint.Value = "Up"
		warn("Unknown Type. Only 4 available: \226\128\156Up\226\128\157, \226\128\156Down\226\128\157, \226\128\156Left\226\128\157 and \226\128\156Right\226\128\157, changing to \226\128\156Up\226\128\157.")
	end
	if script.MissingPartType.Value == "Color" then
		v10.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v11.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v10.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0)
		v11.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0)
		return
	elseif script.MissingPartType.Value == "Trans" then
		v10.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v11.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v10.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1, 1, 1))
		v11.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1, 1, 1))
		return
	elseif script.MissingPartType.Value == "TransAndColor" then
		v10.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v11.UIGradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.TransOfPercentPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value),
			NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.TransOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v10.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
		v11.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, script.ColorOfPercentPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.502, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value),
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, script.ColorOfMissingPart.Value)
		})
	else
		script.MissingPartType.Value = "Trans"
		warn("Unknown Type. Only 3 available: \226\128\156Trans\226\128\157, \226\128\156Color\226\128\157 and \226\128\156TransAndColor\226\128\157, changing to \226\128\156Trans\226\128\157.")
	end
end
Progress(0)
script.Parent:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function()
	Progress(script.Parent.Value)
end)
for _, v17 in pairs(script:GetChildren()) do
	v17:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function()
		Progress(script.Parent.Value)
	end)
end

local function v_u_25() -- name: GetResultTable
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_6
	local v24 = {
		["FullName"] = v_u_21[2],
		["NFT"] = string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[1]
	}
	if string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2] then
		v24.Model = string.split(string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2], ")")[1]
	else
		v24.Model = "Default"
	end
	v24.Owner = v_u_21[3]
	v24.Backdrop = v_u_21[4]
	v24.Color = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_21[4]]
	v24.Pattern = v_u_21[5]
	v24.Date = v_u_21[6]
	v24.Number = v_u_21[7]
	return v24
end
local function v_u_33(p26) -- name: radialprogress
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_5
	local v27 = p26 / 100 * 360
	local v28 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Left.Circle
	local v29 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Right.Circle
	if p26 > 0 and p26 <= 50 then
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = true
		v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + v27
		}):Play()
		return
	elseif p26 <= 0 then
		if v29.UIGradient.Rotation ~= -180 then
			local v30 = v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
				["Rotation"] = -180
			})
			v30:Play()
			v30.Completed:Wait()
		end
		local v31 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180
		})
		v31:Play()
		v31.Completed:Wait()
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = false
	else
		v28.Visible = true
		v29.Visible = true
		local v32 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = 0
		})
		v32:Play()
		v32.Completed:Wait()
		v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + (v27 - 180)
		}):Play()
	end
end
local function v_u_43() -- name: UpdateSelected
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_33
	local v34 = 0
	local v35 = ""
	for v36 = 1, 4 do
		local v37 = v_u_10:FindFirstChild("Frame" .. v36)
		if v_u_16[v36] then
			v37.NFTFrame.NFT.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Image
			for _, v38 in v37.NFTFrame.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				v38.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_14[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Pattern")]
			end
			v37.NFTFrame.BackgroundColor3 = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Backdrop")]
			local v39 = (v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Price or 0) / 320000000
			local v40 = math.clamp(v39, 0, 1) * 20 + 5
			local v41 = math.round(v40)
			v34 = v34 + v41
			v37.NFTFrame.Percent.Text = tostring(v41) .. "%"
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = true
			v35 = string.split(v_u_16[v36].Name, " (")[1]
		else
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = false
		end
	end
	if #v_u_16 <= 0 then
		v_u_22 = nil
		v35 = ""
	end
	local v42 = math.clamp(v34, 0, 100)
	task.spawn(v_u_33, v42)
	v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.percent.Text = tostring(v42) .. "%"
	v_u_10.Button.Succ.Text = "Success Chance: " .. tostring(v42) .. "%"
	if v_u_22 then
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft " .. v35 .. " " .. v_u_22
	else
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft"
	end
end
local function v_u_46(p44) -- name: SelectGift
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_43
	if not table.find(v_u_16, p44) then
		if v_u_16[1] then
			if string.split(v_u_16[1].Name, " (")[1] == string.split(p44.Name, " (")[1] then
				if #v_u_16 < 4 then
					local v45 = v_u_16
					table.insert(v45, p44)
				end
			else
				v_u_16 = { p44 }
				v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
			end
		else
			v_u_16 = { p44 }
			v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
		end
		v_u_43()
	end
end
local function v_u_77(p47) -- name: CraftRoll
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_43, (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_9
	v_u_43()
	if p47[1] == "Failed" then
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.hammer.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.anvil.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.broken.Visible = true
		v_u_10.info2.Text = "<b>Unlucky!</b>\nYou\'ve lost <b>" .. p47[2] .. "</b> gifts."
		v_u_10.Parent.Inventory.Visible = false
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft more"
		v_u_10.Button.Succ.Visible = false
		v_u_17 = false
		return
	elseif p47[1] == "Blessing" then
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.hammer.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.anvil.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.broken.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.safe.Visible = true
		v_u_10.info2.Text = "<b>Saved!</b>\nYour <b>" .. p47[2] .. "</b> gifts were saved by a Blessing."
		v_u_10.Parent.Inventory.Visible = false
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft more"
		v_u_10.Button.Succ.Visible = false
		v_u_17 = false
		v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_4.UI_Cross)
	elseif p47[1] == "Success" then
		local v_u_48 = v_u_25()
		local _ = string.split(v_u_48.FullName, " (")[1]
		v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.05, 0)
		for _, v49 in v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame:GetChildren() do
			if v49:IsA("ImageLabel") then
				v49:Destroy()
			end
		end
		local v50 = {}
		for v51, v52 in pairs(v_u_6.Gifts) do
			if v52.Crafted and string.find(v51, "Desk Calendar") then
				table.insert(v50, v51)
			end
		end
		for v53 = 1, 42 do
			local v54 = script.Icon:Clone()
			v54.Parent = v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame
			v54.LayoutOrder = v53
			if v53 == 41 then
				v54.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_48.FullName].Image
				v54.Name = "Yes"
			else
				local v55 = v50[math.random(1, #v50)]
				v54.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v55].Image
			end
		end
		v_u_12.Visible = true
		v_u_5:Create(v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame, TweenInfo.new(5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
			["Position"] = UDim2.new(-13, 0, 0.05, 0)
		}):Play()
		for _, v_u_56 in v_u_13:GetDescendants() do
			if v_u_56:IsA("TextLabel") and v_u_48[v_u_56.Name] then
				task.spawn(function()
					-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_48, (copy) v_u_56
					local v57 = v_u_48[v_u_56.Name]
					local v58 = 5 / string.len(v57)
					for v59 = 1, string.len(v57) do
						local v60 = string.sub(v57, 1, v59)
						v_u_56.Text = v60 .. string.rep("?", string.len(v57) - string.len(v60))
						task.wait(v58)
					end
				end)
			end
		end
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_17, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_48
			for _ = 1, 9 do
				if not v_u_17 then
					return
				end
				local v61 = v_u_5
				local v62 = v_u_13.TopFrame
				local v63 = TweenInfo.new(0.5)
				local v64 = v_u_6.Backdrops
				local v65 = {}
				local v66 = {}
				for v67, _ in v_u_6.Backdrops do
					table.insert(v65, v67)
				end
				v66.BackgroundColor3 = v64[v65[math.random(1, #v65)]]
				v61:Create(v62, v63, v66):Play()
				local v68 = v_u_6.Patterns
				local v69 = {}
				for v70, _ in v_u_6.Patterns do
					table.insert(v69, v70)
				end
				local v71 = v68[v69[math.random(1, #v69)]]
				for _, v72 in v_u_13.TopFrame.Patterns:GetChildren() do
					if v72:IsA("ImageLabel") then
						v72.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v71
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
			end
			v_u_5:Create(v_u_13.TopFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {
				["BackgroundColor3"] = v_u_48.Color
			}):Play()
			for _, v73 in v_u_13.TopFrame.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				if v73:IsA("ImageLabel") then
					v73.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Patterns[v_u_48.Pattern]
				end
			end
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_17, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
			local v74 = tick()
			local v75 = 0.1
			while tick() - v74 < 5 do
				if not v_u_17 then
					return
				end
				v75 = v75 * 1.1
				v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_4.UI_Tick, v_u_9)
				task.wait(v75)
			end
		end)
		task.wait(5.5)
		for _, v76 in v_u_13.TopFrame.RollFrame:GetChildren() do
			if v76:IsA("ImageLabel") and v76.Name ~= "Yes" then
				v_u_5:Create(v76, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {
					["ImageTransparency"] = 1
				}):Play()
			end
		end
	end
end
function TableFormat(p78, p79) -- name: TableFormat
	local v80 = {}
	for v81, v82 in ipairs(p78) do
		if v81 ~= p79 then
			table.insert(v80, v82)
		end
	end
	return v80
end
local v_u_83 = v_u_22
local v_u_84 = v_u_21
local v_u_85 = v_u_20

	v_u_89:WaitForChild("Button").Activated:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_87, (ref) v_u_86, (copy) v_u_88, (copy) v_u_43, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_89
		if not v_u_87 then
			if v_u_86[v_u_88] then
				v_u_86 = TableFormat(v_u_86, v_u_88)
				v_u_43()
				v_u_5:Create(v_u_89.Delete, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
					["ImageTransparency"] = 1
				}):Play()
			end
		end
	end)
	v_u_89.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_86, (copy) v_u_88, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_89
		if v_u_86[v_u_88] then
			v_u_5:Create(v_u_89.Delete, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
				["ImageTransparency"] = 0.3
			}):Play()
		end
	end)
	v_u_89.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_89
		v_u_5:Create(v_u_89.Delete, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
			["ImageTransparency"] = 1
		}):Play()
	end)
end
local function v_u_94(p_u_90) -- name: ItemFrame
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_87, (copy) v_u_46
	if p_u_90:GetAttribute("Delay") then
		task.wait(p_u_90:GetAttribute("Delay"))
		if p_u_90.Parent ~= v_u_7 then
			return
		end
	end
	if p_u_90:GetAttribute("Unique") then
		local v91 = p_u_90.Name
		if v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Price >= 10000 then
			local v_u_92 = script.UniqueFrame:Clone()
			v_u_92.Name = p_u_90.Name
			v_u_92.Txt.Text = v91
			v_u_92.Price.Text = "\240\159\146\160 " .. v_u_3.SimpleNumber(v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Price / 250)
			v_u_92.ImageLabel.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Image
			for _, v93 in v_u_92.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				v93.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_14[p_u_90:GetAttribute("Pattern")]
			end
			v_u_92.BackgroundColor3 = v_u_15[p_u_90:GetAttribute("Backdrop")]
			v_u_92.Count.Text = p_u_90:GetAttribute("Number")
			v_u_92.Parent = v_u_11
			v_u_92.Limited.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Limited
			v_u_92.Winter.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_90.Name].Winter
			v_u_92.Summer.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_90.Name].Summer
			p_u_90.Destroying:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_92
				v_u_92:Destroy()
			end)
			v_u_92.Button.Activated:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_87, (ref) v_u_46, (copy) p_u_90
				if not v_u_87 then
					v_u_46(p_u_90)
				end
			end)
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
for _, v95 in v_u_7:GetChildren() do
	if v_u_6.Gifts[v95.Name].Craftable then
		task.spawn(v_u_94, v95)
	end
end

	end
end)
local function v_u_99(p97) -- name: CraftVisualEnd

	}):Play()

	for v98 = 1, 4 do
		v_u_5:Create(v_u_10:FindFirstChild("Frame" .. v98).White, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {
			["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1
		}):Play()
	end
	v_u_85 = task.spawn(v_u_77, p97)
end
local function v_u_115(p100) -- name: CraftVisual
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_86, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_99
	local v101 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.hammer
	local v102 = #v_u_86
	for v103 = 1, v102 do
		local v104 = v_u_10:FindFirstChild("Frame" .. v103)
		local v105 = v104.AbsolutePosition
		v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.15, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
			["Rotation"] = 60
		}):Play()
		local v106 = v101.Parent
		local v107 = v106.AbsolutePosition
		local v108 = v106.AbsoluteSize
		local v109 = (v105.X - v107.X) / v108.X
		local v110 = (v105.Y - v107.Y) / v108.Y
		local v111 = UDim2.new(v109 + 0.425, 0, v110 + 0.258, 0)
		task.wait(0.15)
		v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
			["Position"] = v111
		}):Play()
		task.wait(0.5)
		v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.075, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
			["Rotation"] = 0
		}):Play()
		v_u_3.CreatePitchSound(v_u_4.Craft, 1 - v102 / 10 + v103 * 0.1, v_u_8)
		task.wait(0.075)
		v_u_5:Create(v104.White, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {
			["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0
		}):Play()
		task.wait(0.15)
		v104.NFTFrame.Visible = false
		v_u_5:Create(v104.White, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {
			["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1
		}):Play()
		for _ = 1, math.random(3, 5) do
			local v112 = script.Dot:Clone()
			v112.Position = v104.Position
			v112.ImageColor3 = v104.NFTFrame.BackgroundColor3
			local v113 = math.random(10, 30) / 100
			v112.Size = UDim2.new(v113, 0, v113, 0)
			v112.Parent = v_u_10.Dots
			v_u_5:Create(v112, TweenInfo.new(1.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
				["Position"] = v104.Position + UDim2.new(math.random(-15, 15) / 100, 0, math.random(-15, 15) / 100, 0)
			}):Play()
		end
	end
	task.wait(0.15)
	v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
		["Position"] = UDim2.new(0.55, 0, 0.375, 0)
	}):Play()
	v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.075, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
		["Rotation"] = 60
	}):Play()
	task.wait(0.5)
	v_u_5:Create(v101, TweenInfo.new(0.075, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential), {
		["Rotation"] = 0
	}):Play()
	v_u_3.CreatePitchSound(v_u_4.Craft, 1.1, v_u_8)
	v_u_5:Create(v_u_10.FinalFrame.White, TweenInfo.new(1.5), {
		["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0
	}):Play()
	for _, v_u_114 in v_u_10.Dots:GetChildren() do
		task.delay(math.random(0, 75) / 100, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_114, (ref) v_u_10
			v_u_5:Create(v_u_114, TweenInfo.new(0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
				["Position"] = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Position
			}):Play()
			task.wait(0.5)
			v_u_5:Create(v_u_114, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {
				["ImageTransparency"] = 1
			}):Play()
		end)
	end
	task.wait(2)
	v_u_99(p100)

v_u_10.Button.Activated:Connect(function()

	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_3
	local v11 = 0

		end

v_u_9.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_14
	local v15 = 0
	for _, v16 in v_u_10 do
		v15 = v15 + v16
	end
	if v15 > 10 or v15 < 1 then
		return
	else
		local v17 = {}
		for v18, v19 in v_u_10 do
			for _ = 1, v19 do
				table.insert(v17, v18)
			end
		end
		if #v17 > 10 or #v17 < 1 then
			return
		else
			local v20, v21 = v_u_4.Battles:InvokeServer("Create", v17, {})
			if v20 then
				v_u_7.MainFrame.Visible = false
				v_u_6.Visible = false
				v_u_7:WaitForChild("Battle").Visible = true
				v_u_10 = {}
				for _, v22 in v_u_8:GetChildren() do
					if v22:IsA("Frame") and v22:FindFirstChild("Buttons") then
						v22.Buttons.Selected.Visible = false
					end
				end

				v_u_4.Btl:Fire(v17)
			else
				v_u_3.Notify("ERROR", v21, v_u_5.UI_Error)
			end
		end
	end
end)

			v_u_19 = true

			v_u_5:Create(v_u_20, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Cubic, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
				["Rotation"] = v_u_20.Rotation - 120

				["Rotation"] = v25

			end
			task.wait(1)
			v_u_19 = false
		end
	end
end)

--- PlayerGui/HoverEffect ---
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_2 = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
local v_u_3 = TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
local v4 = script.Parent
function getTweens(p5) -- name: getTweens
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3
	local v6 = p5:GetAttribute("HoverPadding") or 2
	local v7 = p5.Size
	return v_u_1:Create(p5, v_u_2, {
		["Size"] = UDim2.new(v7.X.Scale, v7.X.Offset + v6, v7.Y.Scale, v7.Y.Offset + v6)
	}), v_u_1:Create(p5, v_u_3, {
		["Size"] = v7
	})
end
function handleDescendant(p8) -- name: handleDescendant
	if p8.Name ~= "Profile" or p8.Parent.Name ~= "Right" then
		if p8:IsA("TextButton") or p8:IsA("ImageButton") then
			if p8:GetAttribute("DONT_ANIMATE") then
				return
			end
			local v9
			if p8:FindFirstChild("Container") then
				v9 = p8.Container
			else
				v9 = p8
			end
			local v_u_10, v_u_11 = getTweens(v9)
			local v_u_12 = false
			p8.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_10
				if not v_u_12 then
					v_u_12 = true
					v_u_10:Play()
				end
			end)
			p8.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
			p8.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
		end
	end
end
for _, v13 in pairs(v4:GetDescendants()) do
	handleDescendant(v13)
end
v4.DescendantAdded:Connect(handleDescendant)

--- PlayerGui/Messages/MessageHandler ---
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v2 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local v3 = v2.Remotes.DisplayGlobalAnnouncement
local v_u_4 = v2.Templates.Messages.Message
local v_u_5 = script.Parent.Container
local v_u_6 = TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
local v_u_7 = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
function message_appear(p8) -- name: message_appear
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6
	p8.Background.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	p8.Background.TextLabel.TextTransparency = 1
	p8.Background.TextLabel.UIStroke.Transparency = 1
	v_u_1:Create(p8.Background, v_u_6, {
		["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0
	}):Play()
	v_u_1:Create(p8.Background.TextLabel, v_u_6, {
		["TextTransparency"] = 0
	}):Play()
	v_u_1:Create(p8.Background.TextLabel.UIStroke, v_u_6, {
		["Transparency"] = 0
	}):Play()
end
function message_disappear(p9) -- name: message_disappear
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_7
	v_u_1:Create(p9.Background, v_u_7, {
		["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1,
		["Position"] = nil,
		["Position"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0)
	}):Play()
	v_u_1:Create(p9.Background.TextLabel, v_u_7, {
		["TextTransparency"] = 1
	}):Play()
	local v10 = v_u_1:Create(p9.Background.TextLabel.UIStroke, v_u_7, {
		["Transparency"] = 1
	})
	v10:Play()
	v10.Completed:Wait()
	p9:Destroy()
end
function display_message(p11, p12) -- name: display_message
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_5
	local v13 = v_u_4:Clone()
	v13.Background.TextLabel.Text = p11
	v13.ZIndex = 1000
	message_appear(v13)
	v13.Parent = v_u_5
	script.Sound:Play()
	task.wait(p12)
	message_disappear(v13)
end
v3.OnClientEvent:Connect(display_message)

local function v_u_26(p23, p24) -- name: getRelativeVelocity
	if p23 then
		local v25 = p23.ActiveController and (not (p23.ActiveController:IsA("GroundController") and p23.GroundSensor) and p23.ActiveController:IsA("ClimbController"))
		if v25 then
			v25 = p23.ClimbSensor
		end
		if v25 and v25.SensedPart then
			return p24 - v25.SensedPart:GetVelocityAtPosition(p23.RootPart.Position)
		else
			return p24
		end
	else
		return p24
	end
end
local v_u_103 = v4.new({
	["humanoid"] = "Humanoid",
	["rootPart"] = "HumanoidRootPart"
}, function(p27) -- name: initializeSoundSystem
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_20, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_2
	local v_u_28 = p27.humanoid
	local v_u_29 = p27.rootPart
	local v_u_30 = nil
	local v_u_31
	if v_u_8 then
		v_u_31 = v_u_28.Parent:FindFirstChild("ControllerManager")
	else
		v_u_31 = nil
	end
	local v_u_32 = {}
	if v_u_12 and v_u_3.CharacterSoundsUseNewApi == Enum.RolloutState.Enabled then
		local v33 = nil
		local v34 = nil
		if v_u_16 then
			if v_u_20 then
				v34 = v_u_28.RootPart or v_u_28.Parent
			else
				v34 = v_u_28.RootPart
			end
		else
			v33 = v_u_1.LocalPlayer.Character
		end
		local v35 = 5
		local v36 = {}
		while v35 < 150 do
			v36[v35] = 5 / v35
			v35 = v35 * 1.25
		end

local function v_u_4(p1) -- name: parsePath
	local v2 = string.split(p1, "/")
	for v3 = #v2, 1, -1 do
		if v2[v3] == "" then
			table.remove(v2, v3)
		end
	end
	return v2
end
local function v_u_11(p5, p6) -- name: unbindNodeDescend
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11
	if p5.instance ~= nil then
		p5.instance = nil
		local v7 = p5.connections
		if v7 then
			for _, v8 in ipairs(v7) do
				v8:Disconnect()
			end
			table.clear(v7)
		end
		if p6 and p5.alias then
			p6[p5.alias] = nil
		end
		local v9 = p5.children
		if v9 then
			for _, v10 in pairs(v9) do
				v_u_11(v10, p6)
			end
		end
	end
end
local v_u_12 = {}

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_12

end
function v_u_12._startBoundFn(p24, p25, p26) -- name: _startBoundFn
	local v27 = p24._boundFn
	local v28 = p24._dtorMap

		v29()
		v28[p25] = nil

	if v30 then
		v28[p25] = v30
	end
end
function v_u_12._stopBoundFn(p31, p32) -- name: _stopBoundFn
	local v33 = p31._dtorMap
	local v34 = v33[p32]

		v34()
		v33[p32] = nil

function v_u_12.bindRoot(p_u_35, p_u_36) -- name: bindRoot
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11
	debug.profilebegin("AtomicBinding:BindRoot")
	local v37 = p_u_35._parsedManifest
	local v38 = p_u_35._rootInstToRootNode
	local v39 = p_u_35._rootInstToManifest
	local v_u_40 = p_u_35._manifestSizeTarget
	local v41 = v39[p_u_36] == nil
	assert(v41)
	local v_u_42 = {}
	v39[p_u_36] = v_u_42
	debug.profilebegin("BuildTree")
	local v43 = {
		["alias"] = "root",
		["instance"] = p_u_36
	}
	if next(v37) then
		v43.children = {}
		v43.connections = {}
	end
	v38[p_u_36] = v43
	for v44, v45 in pairs(v37) do
		local v46 = v43
		for v47, v48 in ipairs(v45) do
			local v49 = v47 == #v45
			local v50 = v43.children[v48] or {}
			if v49 then
				if v50.alias ~= nil then
					error("Multiple aliases assigned to one instance")
				end
				v50.alias = v44
			else
				v50.children = v50.children or {}
				v50.connections = v50.connections or {}
			end
			v43.children[v48] = v50
			v43 = v50
		end
		v43 = v46
	end
	debug.profileend()
	local function v_u_77(p51) -- name: processNode
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_42, (copy) v_u_77, (copy) p_u_35, (copy) p_u_36, (ref) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_40
		local v52 = p51.instance
		local v_u_53 = assert(v52)
		local v_u_54 = p51.children
		local v55 = p51.alias
		local v56 = not v_u_54
		if v55 then
			v_u_42[v55] = v_u_53
		end
		if not v56 then
			local function v59(p57) -- name: processAddChild
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_54, (ref) v_u_77
				local v58 = v_u_54[p57.Name]

					v58.instance = p57

				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_54, (ref) p_u_35, (ref) p_u_36, (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_42, (copy) v_u_53, (ref) v_u_77

						p_u_35:_stopBoundFn(p_u_36)

						assert(v63)
						local v64 = v_u_53:FindFirstChild(v61)
						local v65 = v64 and v_u_54[v64.Name]
						if v65 then
							if v65.instance ~= nil then
								return
							end
							v65.instance = v64
							v_u_77(v65)
						end
					end
				else
					return
				end
			end
			for _, v67 in ipairs(v_u_53:GetChildren()) do
				local v68 = v_u_54[v67.Name]
				if v68 then
					if v68.instance == nil then
						v68.instance = v67
						v_u_77(v68)
					end
				end
			end
			local v69 = p51.connections
			local v70 = v_u_53.ChildAdded
			table.insert(v69, v70:Connect(v59))
			local v71 = p51.connections
			local v72 = v_u_53.ChildRemoved
			table.insert(v71, v72:Connect(v66))
		end
		if v56 then
			local v73 = v_u_42
			local v74 = v_u_40
			local v75 = 0
			for _ in pairs(v73) do
				v75 = v75 + 1
			end

			assert(v76, v75)
			if v75 == v74 then
				p_u_35:_startBoundFn(p_u_36, v_u_42)
			end
		end
	end

	v_u_77(v43)
	debug.profileend()
	debug.profileend()
end
function v_u_12.unbindRoot(p78, p79) -- name: unbindRoot
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11
	local v80 = p78._rootInstToRootNode
	local v81 = p78._rootInstToManifest
	p78:_stopBoundFn(p79)
	local v82 = v80[p79]
	if v82 then
		local v83 = v81[p79]
		v_u_11(v82, (assert(v83)))
		v80[p79] = nil
	end
	v81[p79] = nil
end
function v_u_12.destroy(p84) -- name: destroy
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11
	debug.profilebegin("AtomicBinding:destroy")
	for _, v85 in pairs(p84._dtorMap) do
		v85:destroy()
	end
	table.clear(p84._dtorMap)
	for _, v86 in ipairs(p84._connections) do
		v86:Disconnect()
	end
	table.clear(p84._connections)
	local v87 = p84._rootInstToManifest
	for v88, v89 in pairs(p84._rootInstToRootNode) do
		local v90 = v87[v88]
		v_u_11(v89, (assert(v90)))
	end
	table.clear(p84._rootInstToManifest)
	table.clear(p84._rootInstToRootNode)

end
return v_u_12

local v_u_23 = require(script:WaitForChild("MouseLockController"))
local v_u_24 = {}
local v_u_25 = {}
if not v_u_4.LocalPlayer then
	return {}
end
local v26 = v_u_4.LocalPlayer
assert(v26, "Strict typing check")
local v27 = v_u_4.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerScripts")
v27:RegisterTouchCameraMovementMode(Enum.TouchCameraMovementMode.Default)
v27:RegisterTouchCameraMovementMode(Enum.TouchCameraMovementMode.Follow)
v27:RegisterTouchCameraMovementMode(Enum.TouchCameraMovementMode.Classic)
v27:RegisterComputerCameraMovementMode(Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Default)
v27:RegisterComputerCameraMovementMode(Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Follow)
v27:RegisterComputerCameraMovementMode(Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Classic)
v27:RegisterComputerCameraMovementMode(Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.CameraToggle)
local v_u_28 = v11.getUserFlag("UserPlayerConnectionMemoryLeak")
local v_u_29 = v11.getUserFlag("UserPSFixCameraControllerReset")
function v_u_1.new() -- name: new
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_28, (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_6
	local v30 = {
		["activeTransparencyController"] = v_u_22.new()
	}
	local v31
	if v_u_28 then
		v31 = v_u_10.new()
	else
		v31 = nil
	end
	v30.connectionUtil = v31
	local v32 = v_u_1
	local v_u_33 = setmetatable(v30, v32)
	v_u_33.activeCameraController = nil
	v_u_33.activeOcclusionModule = nil
	v_u_33.activeMouseLockController = nil
	v_u_33.currentComputerCameraMovementMode = nil
	v_u_33.cameraSubjectChangedConn = nil
	v_u_33.cameraTypeChangedConn = nil
	for _, v34 in pairs(v_u_4:GetPlayers()) do
		v_u_33:OnPlayerAdded(v34)
	end
	v_u_4.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(p35)
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
		v_u_33:OnPlayerAdded(p35)
	end)
	if v_u_28 then
		v_u_4.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(p36)
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
			v_u_33:OnPlayerRemoving(p36)
		end)
	end
	v_u_33.activeTransparencyController:Enable(true)
	v_u_33.activeMouseLockController = v_u_23.new()
	local v37 = v_u_33.activeMouseLockController
	assert(v37, "Strict typing check")
	local v38 = v_u_33.activeMouseLockController:GetBindableToggleEvent()
	if v38 then
		v38:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
			v_u_33:OnMouseLockToggled()
		end)
	end
	v_u_33:ActivateCameraController()
	v_u_33:ActivateOcclusionModule(v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevCameraOcclusionMode)
	v_u_33:OnCurrentCameraChanged()
	v_u_5:BindToRenderStep("cameraRenderUpdate", Enum.RenderPriority.Camera.Value, function(p39)
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
		v_u_33:Update(p39)
	end)
	for _, v_u_40 in pairs(v_u_2) do
		v_u_4.LocalPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal(v_u_40):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_40
			v_u_33:OnLocalPlayerCameraPropertyChanged(v_u_40)
		end)
	end
	for _, v_u_41 in pairs(v_u_3) do
		v_u_8:GetPropertyChangedSignal(v_u_41):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_41
			v_u_33:OnUserGameSettingsPropertyChanged(v_u_41)
		end)
	end
	game.Workspace:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CurrentCamera"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
		v_u_33:OnCurrentCameraChanged()
	end)
	v_u_6:GetPropertyChangedSignal("PreferredInput"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_33
		v_u_33:OnPreferredInputChanged()
	end)
	return v_u_33
end
function v_u_1.GetCameraMovementModeFromSettings(_) -- name: GetCameraMovementModeFromSettings
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8
	if v_u_4.LocalPlayer.CameraMode == Enum.CameraMode.LockFirstPerson then
		return v_u_12.ConvertCameraModeEnumToStandard(Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Classic)
	else
		local v42, v43
		if v_u_6.PreferredInput == Enum.PreferredInput.Touch then
			v42 = v_u_12.ConvertCameraModeEnumToStandard(v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevTouchCameraMode)
			v43 = v_u_12.ConvertCameraModeEnumToStandard(v_u_8.TouchCameraMovementMode)
		else
			v42 = v_u_12.ConvertCameraModeEnumToStandard(v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevComputerCameraMode)
			v43 = v_u_12.ConvertCameraModeEnumToStandard(v_u_8.ComputerCameraMovementMode)
		end
		if v42 == Enum.DevComputerCameraMovementMode.UserChoice then
			return v43
		else
			return v42
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.ActivateOcclusionModule(p44, p45) -- name: ActivateOcclusionModule
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_20, (copy) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_4
	local v46
	if p45 == Enum.DevCameraOcclusionMode.Zoom then
		v46 = v_u_21
	else
		if p45 ~= Enum.DevCameraOcclusionMode.Invisicam then
			warn("CameraScript ActivateOcclusionModule called with unsupported mode")
			return
		end
		v46 = v_u_20
	end
	p44.occlusionMode = p45
	if p44.activeOcclusionModule and p44.activeOcclusionModule:GetOcclusionMode() == p45 then
		if not p44.activeOcclusionModule:GetEnabled() then
			p44.activeOcclusionModule:Enable(true)
		end
	else
		local v47 = p44.activeOcclusionModule
		p44.activeOcclusionModule = v_u_25[v46]
		if not p44.activeOcclusionModule then
			p44.activeOcclusionModule = v46.new()
			if p44.activeOcclusionModule then
				v_u_25[v46] = p44.activeOcclusionModule
			end
		end
		if p44.activeOcclusionModule then
			if p44.activeOcclusionModule:GetOcclusionMode() ~= p45 then
				warn("CameraScript ActivateOcclusionModule mismatch: ", p44.activeOcclusionModule:GetOcclusionMode(), "~=", p45)
			end
			if v47 then
				if v47 == p44.activeOcclusionModule then
					warn("CameraScript ActivateOcclusionModule failure to detect already running correct module")
				else
					v47:Enable(false)
				end
			end
			if p45 == Enum.DevCameraOcclusionMode.Invisicam then
				if v_u_4.LocalPlayer.Character then
					p44.activeOcclusionModule:CharacterAdded(v_u_4.LocalPlayer.Character, v_u_4.LocalPlayer)
				end
			else
				for _, v48 in pairs(v_u_4:GetPlayers()) do
					if v48 and v48.Character then
						p44.activeOcclusionModule:CharacterAdded(v48.Character, v48)
					end
				end
				p44.activeOcclusionModule:OnCameraSubjectChanged(game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject)
			end
			p44.activeOcclusionModule:Enable(true)
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.ShouldUseVehicleCamera(p49) -- name: ShouldUseVehicleCamera
	local v50 = workspace.CurrentCamera
	if not v50 then
		return false
	end
	local v51 = v50.CameraType
	local v52 = v50.CameraSubject
	local v53 = v51 == Enum.CameraType.Custom and true or v51 == Enum.CameraType.Follow
	local v54 = v52 and v52:IsA("VehicleSeat") or false
	local v55 = p49.occlusionMode ~= Enum.DevCameraOcclusionMode.Invisicam
	if v54 then
		if not v53 then
			v55 = v53
		end
	else
		v55 = v54
	end
	return v55
end
function v_u_1.ActivateCameraController(p56) -- name: ActivateCameraController
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_19, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_29
	local v57 = workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraType
	local v58 = p56:GetCameraMovementModeFromSettings()
	local v59 = nil
	if v57 == Enum.CameraType.Scriptable then
		if p56.activeCameraController then
			p56.activeCameraController:Enable(false)
			p56.activeCameraController = nil
		end
	else
		if v57 == Enum.CameraType.Custom then
			v58 = p56:GetCameraMovementModeFromSettings()
		elseif v57 == Enum.CameraType.Track then
			v58 = Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Classic
		elseif v57 == Enum.CameraType.Follow then
			v58 = Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Follow
		elseif v57 == Enum.CameraType.Orbital then
			v58 = Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Orbital
		elseif v57 == Enum.CameraType.Attach or (v57 == Enum.CameraType.Watch or v57 == Enum.CameraType.Fixed) then
			v59 = v_u_16
		else
			warn("CameraScript encountered an unhandled Camera.CameraType value: ", v57)
		end
		if not v59 then
			if v_u_7.VREnabled then
				v59 = v_u_18
			elseif v58 == Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Classic or (v58 == Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Follow or (v58 == Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Default or v58 == Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.CameraToggle)) then
				v59 = v_u_14
			else
				if v58 ~= Enum.ComputerCameraMovementMode.Orbital then
					warn("ActivateCameraController did not select a module.")
					return
				end
				v59 = v_u_15
			end
		end
		if p56:ShouldUseVehicleCamera() then
			if v_u_7.VREnabled then
				v59 = v_u_19
			else
				v59 = v_u_17
			end
		end
		local v60
		if v_u_24[v59] then
			v60 = v_u_24[v59]
			if v_u_29 then
				if v60.Reset and p56.activeCameraController ~= v60 then
					v60:Reset()
				end
			elseif v60.Reset then
				v60:Reset()
			end
		else
			v60 = v59.new()
			v_u_24[v59] = v60
		end
		if p56.activeCameraController then
			if p56.activeCameraController == v60 then
				if not p56.activeCameraController:GetEnabled() then
					p56.activeCameraController:Enable(true)
				end
			else
				p56.activeCameraController:Enable(false)
				p56.activeCameraController = v60
				p56.activeCameraController:Enable(true)
			end
		elseif v60 ~= nil then
			p56.activeCameraController = v60
			local v61 = p56.activeCameraController
			assert(v61, "Strict typing check")
			p56.activeCameraController:Enable(true)
		end
		if p56.activeCameraController then
			p56.activeCameraController:SetCameraMovementMode(v58)
			p56.activeCameraController:SetCameraType(v57)
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnCameraSubjectChanged(p62) -- name: OnCameraSubjectChanged
	local v63 = workspace.CurrentCamera
	local v64
	if v63 then
		v64 = v63.CameraSubject
	else
		v64 = nil
	end
	if p62.activeTransparencyController then
		p62.activeTransparencyController:SetSubject(v64)
	end
	if p62.activeOcclusionModule then
		p62.activeOcclusionModule:OnCameraSubjectChanged(v64)
	end
	p62:ActivateCameraController()
end
function v_u_1.OnCameraTypeChanged(p65, p66) -- name: OnCameraTypeChanged
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_12
	if p66 == Enum.CameraType.Scriptable and v_u_6.MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then
		v_u_12.restoreMouseBehavior()
	end
	p65:ActivateCameraController()
end
function v_u_1.OnCurrentCameraChanged(p_u_67) -- name: OnCurrentCameraChanged
	local v_u_68 = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
	if v_u_68 then
		if p_u_67.cameraSubjectChangedConn then
			p_u_67.cameraSubjectChangedConn:Disconnect()
		end
		if p_u_67.cameraTypeChangedConn then
			p_u_67.cameraTypeChangedConn:Disconnect()
		end
		p_u_67.cameraSubjectChangedConn = v_u_68:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CameraSubject"):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_67
			p_u_67:OnCameraSubjectChanged()
		end)
		p_u_67.cameraTypeChangedConn = v_u_68:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CameraType"):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_67, (copy) v_u_68
			p_u_67:OnCameraTypeChanged(v_u_68.CameraType)
		end)
		p_u_67:OnCameraSubjectChanged()
		p_u_67:OnCameraTypeChanged(v_u_68.CameraType)
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnLocalPlayerCameraPropertyChanged(p69, p70) -- name: OnLocalPlayerCameraPropertyChanged
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4
	if p70 == "CameraMode" then
		if v_u_4.LocalPlayer.CameraMode ~= Enum.CameraMode.LockFirstPerson then
			if v_u_4.LocalPlayer.CameraMode == Enum.CameraMode.Classic then
				p69:ActivateCameraController()
			else
				warn("Unhandled value for property player.CameraMode: ", v_u_4.LocalPlayer.CameraMode)
			end
		end
		if not p69.activeCameraController or p69.activeCameraController:GetModuleName() ~= "ClassicCamera" then
			p69:ActivateCameraController()
		end
		if p69.activeCameraController then
			p69.activeCameraController:UpdateForDistancePropertyChange()
			return
		end
	else
		if p70 == "DevComputerCameraMode" or p70 == "DevTouchCameraMode" then
			p69:ActivateCameraController()
			return
		end
		if p70 == "DevCameraOcclusionMode" then
			p69:ActivateOcclusionModule(v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevCameraOcclusionMode)
			return
		end
		if p70 == "CameraMinZoomDistance" or p70 == "CameraMaxZoomDistance" then
			if p69.activeCameraController then
				p69.activeCameraController:UpdateForDistancePropertyChange()
				return
			end
		else
			if p70 == "DevTouchMovementMode" then
				return
			end
			if p70 == "DevComputerMovementMode" then
				return
			end
			local _ = p70 == "DevEnableMouseLock"
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnUserGameSettingsPropertyChanged(p71, p72) -- name: OnUserGameSettingsPropertyChanged
	if p72 == "ComputerCameraMovementMode" or p72 == "TouchCameraMovementMode" then
		p71:ActivateCameraController()
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnPreferredInputChanged(p73) -- name: OnPreferredInputChanged
	p73:ActivateCameraController()
end
function v_u_1.Update(p74, p75) -- name: Update
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_13
	if p74.activeCameraController then
		p74.activeCameraController:UpdateMouseBehavior()
		local v76, v77 = p74.activeCameraController:Update(p75)
		if p74.activeOcclusionModule then
			v76, v77 = p74.activeOcclusionModule:Update(p75, v76, v77)
		end
		local v78 = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
		v78.CFrame = v76
		v78.Focus = v77
		if p74.activeTransparencyController then
			p74.activeTransparencyController:Update(p75)
		end
		if v_u_13.getInputEnabled() then
			v_u_13.resetInputForFrameEnd()
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnCharacterAdded(p79, p80, p81) -- name: OnCharacterAdded
	if p79.activeOcclusionModule then
		p79.activeOcclusionModule:CharacterAdded(p80, p81)
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnCharacterRemoving(p82, p83, p84) -- name: OnCharacterRemoving
	if p82.activeOcclusionModule then
		p82.activeOcclusionModule:CharacterRemoving(p83, p84)
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnPlayerAdded(p_u_85, p_u_86) -- name: OnPlayerAdded
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_28
	if v_u_28 then
		if p_u_85.connectionUtil then
			p_u_85.connectionUtil:trackConnection(("%*CharacterAdded"):format(p_u_86.UserId), p_u_86.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(p87)
				-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_85, (copy) p_u_86
				p_u_85:OnCharacterAdded(p87, p_u_86)
			end))
			p_u_85.connectionUtil:trackConnection(("%*CharacterRemoving"):format(p_u_86.UserId), p_u_86.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function(p88)
				-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_85, (copy) p_u_86
				p_u_85:OnCharacterRemoving(p88, p_u_86)
			end))
			return
		end
	else
		p_u_86.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(p89)
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_85, (copy) p_u_86
			p_u_85:OnCharacterAdded(p89, p_u_86)
		end)
		p_u_86.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function(p90)
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_85, (copy) p_u_86
			p_u_85:OnCharacterRemoving(p90, p_u_86)
		end)
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnPlayerRemoving(p91, p92) -- name: OnPlayerRemoving
	if p91.connectionUtil then
		p91.connectionUtil:disconnect((("%*CharacterAdded"):format(p92.UserId)))
		p91.connectionUtil:disconnect((("%*CharacterRemoving"):format(p92.UserId)))
	end
end
function v_u_1.OnMouseLockToggled(p93) -- name: OnMouseLockToggled
	if p93.activeMouseLockController then
		local v94 = p93.activeMouseLockController:GetIsMouseLocked()
		local v95 = p93.activeMouseLockController:GetMouseLockOffset()
		if p93.activeCameraController then
			p93.activeCameraController:SetIsMouseLocked(v94)
			p93.activeCameraController:SetMouseLockOffset(v95)
		end
	end
end
v_u_1.new()
return {}

--- PlayerScripts/PlayerModule/CameraModule/MouseLockController ---
local v1 = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("CommonUtils")
local v2 = require(v1:WaitForChild("FlagUtil"))
local v_u_3 = Enum.ContextActionPriority.Medium.Value
local v_u_4 = game:GetService("Players")
local v_u_5 = game:GetService("ContextActionService")
local v_u_6 = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local v_u_7 = UserSettings().GameSettings
local v_u_8 = require(script.Parent:WaitForChild("CameraUtils"))
local v_u_9 = v2.getUserFlag("UserFixStuckShiftLock")
local v_u_10 = {}
v_u_10.__index = v_u_10
function v_u_10.new() -- name: new
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_6
	local v11 = v_u_10
	local v_u_12 = setmetatable({}, v11)
	v_u_12.isMouseLocked = false
	v_u_12.savedMouseCursor = nil
	v_u_12.boundKeys = { Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift, Enum.KeyCode.RightShift }
	v_u_12.mouseLockToggledEvent = Instance.new("BindableEvent")
	local v13 = script:FindFirstChild("BoundKeys")
	if not (v13 and v13:IsA("StringValue")) then
		if v13 then
			v13:Destroy()
		end
		v13 = Instance.new("StringValue")
		assert(v13, "")
		v13.Name = "BoundKeys"
		v13.Value = "LeftShift,RightShift"
		v13.Parent = script
	end
	if v13 then
		v13.Changed:Connect(function(p14)
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12
			v_u_12:OnBoundKeysObjectChanged(p14)
		end)
		v_u_12:OnBoundKeysObjectChanged(v13.Value)
	end
	v_u_7.Changed:Connect(function(p15)
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12
		if p15 == "ControlMode" or p15 == "ComputerMovementMode" then
			v_u_12:UpdateMouseLockAvailability()
		end
	end)
	v_u_4.LocalPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal("DevEnableMouseLock"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12
		v_u_12:UpdateMouseLockAvailability()
	end)
	v_u_4.LocalPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal("DevComputerMovementMode"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12
		v_u_12:UpdateMouseLockAvailability()
	end)
	v_u_6:GetPropertyChangedSignal("PreferredInput"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12
		v_u_12:UpdateMouseLockAvailability()
	end)
	v_u_12:UpdateMouseLockAvailability()
	return v_u_12
end
function v_u_10.GetIsMouseLocked(p16) -- name: GetIsMouseLocked
	return p16.isMouseLocked
end
function v_u_10.GetBindableToggleEvent(p17) -- name: GetBindableToggleEvent
	return p17.mouseLockToggledEvent.Event
end
function v_u_10.GetMouseLockOffset(_) -- name: GetMouseLockOffset
	return Vector3.new(1.75, 0, 0)
end
function v_u_10.UpdateMouseLockAvailability(p18) -- name: UpdateMouseLockAvailability
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6
	local v19 = v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevEnableMouseLock
	local v20 = v_u_4.LocalPlayer.DevComputerMovementMode == Enum.DevComputerMovementMode.Scriptable
	local v21 = v_u_7.ControlMode == Enum.ControlMode.MouseLockSwitch
	local v22 = v_u_7.ComputerMovementMode == Enum.ComputerMovementMode.ClickToMove
	local v23 = v_u_6.PreferredInput == Enum.PreferredInput.KeyboardAndMouse and (v19 and (v21 and not v22))
	if v23 then
		v23 = not v20
	end
	if v23 ~= p18.enabled then
		p18:EnableMouseLock(v23)
	end
end
function v_u_10.OnBoundKeysObjectChanged(p24, p25) -- name: OnBoundKeysObjectChanged
	p24.boundKeys = {}
	for v26 in string.gmatch(p25, "[^%s,]+") do
		for _, v27 in pairs(Enum.KeyCode:GetEnumItems()) do
			if v26 == v27.Name then
				p24.boundKeys[#p24.boundKeys + 1] = v27
				break
			end
		end
	end
	p24:UnbindContextActions()
	p24:BindContextActions()
end
function v_u_10.OnMouseLockToggled(p28) -- name: OnMouseLockToggled
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
	p28.isMouseLocked = not p28.isMouseLocked
	if p28.isMouseLocked then
		local v29 = script:FindFirstChild("CursorImage")
		if v29 and (v29:IsA("StringValue") and v29.Value) then
			v_u_8.setMouseIconOverride(v29.Value)
		else
			if v29 then
				v29:Destroy()
			end
			local v30 = Instance.new("StringValue")
			assert(v30, "")
			v30.Name = "CursorImage"
			v30.Value = "rbxasset://textures/MouseLockedCursor.png"
			v30.Parent = script
			v_u_8.setMouseIconOverride("rbxasset://textures/MouseLockedCursor.png")
		end
	else
		v_u_8.restoreMouseIcon()
	end
	p28.mouseLockToggledEvent:Fire()
end
function v_u_10.DoMouseLockSwitch(p31, _, p32, _) -- name: DoMouseLockSwitch
	if p32 ~= Enum.UserInputState.Begin then
		return Enum.ContextActionResult.Pass
	end
	p31:OnMouseLockToggled()
	return Enum.ContextActionResult.Sink
end
function v_u_10.BindContextActions(p_u_33) -- name: BindContextActions
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_3
	local v34 = v_u_5
	local v35 = v_u_3
	local v36 = p_u_33.boundKeys
	v34:BindActionAtPriority("MouseLockSwitchAction", function(p37, p38, p39)
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_33
		return p_u_33:DoMouseLockSwitch(p37, p38, p39)
	end, false, v35, unpack(v36))
end
function v_u_10.UnbindContextActions(_) -- name: UnbindContextActions
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5
	v_u_5:UnbindAction("MouseLockSwitchAction")
end
function v_u_10.IsMouseLocked(p40) -- name: IsMouseLocked
	local v41 = p40.enabled
	if v41 then
		v41 = p40.isMouseLocked
	end
	return v41
end
function v_u_10.EnableMouseLock(p42, p43) -- name: EnableMouseLock
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_9
	if p43 ~= p42.enabled then
		p42.enabled = p43
		if p42.enabled then
			p42:BindContextActions()
			return
		end
		v_u_8.restoreMouseIcon()
		p42:UnbindContextActions()
		if v_u_9 then
			if p42.isMouseLocked then
				p42.isMouseLocked = false
				p42.mouseLockToggledEvent:Fire()
				return
			end
		else
			if p42.isMouseLocked then
				p42.mouseLockToggledEvent:Fire()
			end
			p42.isMouseLocked = false
		end
	end
end
return v_u_10

--- PlayerScripts/PlayerModule/CameraModule/VRBaseCamera ---
local v1, v2 = pcall(function()
	return UserSettings():IsUserFeatureEnabled("UserVRVehicleCamera2")

local v_u_3 = v1 and v2
local v_u_4 = game:GetService("VRService")

function v_u_13.new() -- name: new

	v16.gamepadZoomLevels = { 0, 7 }
	v16.headScale = 1

	v16.VRFadeResetTimer = 0
	v16.VREdgeBlurTimer = 0

function v_u_13.Reset(p17) -- name: Reset

function v_u_13.GetModuleName(_) -- name: GetModuleName

function v_u_13.GamepadZoomPress(p18) -- name: GamepadZoomPress

	p18:GamepadReset()
	p18:ResetZoom()

	p19.stepRotateTimeout = 0
	p19.needsReset = true
